### [123] [Resilience Characterization of AI-Native Wireless Receivers via Persistent Homology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22886)
*Christo Kurisummoottil Thomas,Emilio Calvanese Strinati*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出拓扑韧性指数（TRI），用于实时评估深度学习无线接收机在非平稳信道下的分布偏移韧性，并在仿真中显示其比梯度范数和验证损失基线更早预警且能指导再适应降低BER。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统BER等指标难以及时刻画AI原生无线接收机在信道分布变化、在线适应过程中的韧性与失效风险，因此需要一种可实时监控、对分布偏移敏感且具有理论稳定性的度量。

Method: 作者基于持久同调与持久性指数构建TRI，综合三部分：验证损失韧性（损失景观子水平集的拓扑持久性）、CIR分布偏移（相对校准参考分布的几何漂移）、信道流形拓扑（高斯核矩阵谱隙并用Ollivier-Ricci曲率范数归一化）。同时证明TRI有界、随性能退化单调、对Wasserstein距离扰动Lipschitz稳定。

Result: 在OFDM深度学习接收机跨十种ITU-R环境转换、三种偏移速率的仿真中，TRI相较梯度范数和验证损失基线提供超过一个OFDM符号的平均预警提前量；梯度范数基线在所有场景中预警提前量为零。TRI引导的突发再适应在200个OFDM符号内使偏移后BER相较不适应降低80%。

Conclusion: TRI为非平稳无线环境中的AI接收机提供了可解释、实时、拓扑稳定的韧性评估工具，并可用于触发自适应策略以改善偏移后的通信可靠性。

Abstract: AI-native wireless receivers based on deep learning exhibit remarkable performance under stationary channel conditions, yet their resilience to distributional shifts remains poorly characterized by conventional metrics such as bit error rate (BER). To overcome these limitations, this paper proposes a novel real-time metric, the Topological Resilience Index (TRI), grounded in persistent homology and persistence exponents. TRI quantifies the structural stability of a neural network receiver's parameter space during online adaptation to non-stationary channels. Specifically, TRI captures resilience through three complementary dimensions: (i) validation-loss resilience measuring model-channel mismatch, grounded in the topological persistence of loss-landscape sublevel sets; (ii) channel impulse response (CIR) distribution shift, tracking geometric drift of CIR vectors from the calibration reference distribution; and (iii) channel manifold topology, quantified by the spectral gap of the Gaussian kernel matrix normalized by the Olivier-Ricci curvature norm. We establish theoretical guarantees showing that TRI is bounded, monotonic under performance degradation, and Lipschitz-stable with respect to perturbations in channel distributions measured in Wasserstein distance. Simulation results for an OFDM deep-learning receiver adapting across ten ITU-R inter-environment transitions at three shift rates demonstrate that TRI provides a consistent mean warning lead of more than one OFDM symbol over gradient-norm and validation-loss baselines, whereas the gradient-norm baseline achieves zero lead in every scenario. Furthermore, the proposed TRI-guided burst re-adaptation reduces post-shift BER by 80% relative to no adaptation within 200 OFDM symbols.

</details>


### [124] [On Reed-Muller subcodes, Grassmannian partitions and sum-free functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22958)
*Philipp Heering,Christian Kaspers,Vladislav Taranchuk*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文将高阶 sum-free 函数与 Reed-Muller 码的线性子码建立等价关系，并给出存在性必要条件、参数下界及其在 Grassmann 图着色/子空间码划分中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Carlet 提出了 k 阶 sum-free 函数并给出构造，但其结构性质、存在条件及与编码理论对象之间的关系仍需深入理解。论文旨在刻画这类函数，并利用其性质产生新的 Reed-Muller 子码与组合设计/图着色结果。

Method: 作者证明在 2≤k≤n−2 且 m≤n 的范围内，非退化的 F₂^m 值 k 阶 sum-free 函数存在，当且仅当 Reed-Muller 码 RM(n−k,n) 存在一个余维 m、最小距离为 3·2^{k−1} 的线性子码；同时推导存在性的必要条件，并分析由该函数诱导的 Grassmannian 划分。

Result: 得到一族新的 Reed-Muller 子码，它们避开 RM(n−k,n) 的所有最小重量码字，最小距离达到原码最小距离的 3/2 倍；给出关于 m 的首个非平凡下界；并在多重 k 阶 sum-free 假设下改进 Grassmannian 划分，强化 Grassmann 图色数上界。

Conclusion: 论文揭示了高阶 sum-free 函数、Reed-Muller 子码、常维子空间码与 Grassmann 图着色之间的深层联系，为构造高距离子码和研究有限几何中的划分问题提供了新的统一框架。

Abstract: A function $F:\mathbb{F}_{2}^{n}\to \mathbb{F}_{2}^{m}$ is called $k$th-order sum-free if the sum of its values over any $k$-dimensional affine subspace of $\mathbb{F}_2^n$ is non-zero. Carlet recently introduced this notion and constructed such functions for every $2\le k\le n$. We prove that, for $2\le k\le n-2$ and $m \leq n$, the existence of a (non-degenerate) $\mathbb{F}_{2}^{m}$-valued $k$th-order sum-free function on $\mathbb{F}_{2}^{n}$ is equivalent to the existence of a codimension $m$ linear subcode of the Reed-Muller code $\mathrm{RM}(n-k,n)$ with minimum distance $3\cdot 2^{k-1}$. In particular, this yields a new family of Reed-Muller subcodes that avoid all minimum weight codewords of $\mathrm{RM}(n-k,n)$, and thus have minimum distance $3/2$ times that of $\mathrm{RM}(n-k,n)$. We also derive new necessary conditions for the existence of $k$th-order sum-free functions and present the first nontrivial lower bound on $m$. Finally, we observe that $k$th-order sum-free functions lead to a partition of the Grassmannian of all $k$-dimensional (linear) subspaces of $\mathbb{F}_2^n$ into constant-dimension subspace codes. Under the assumption that functions exist that are $k$th-order sum-free for multiple values of $k$, we obtain an improved partitioning result and a stronger upper bound on the chromatic number of the Grassmann graphs.

</details>


### [125] [Improved Torn Paper Coding via Local Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23076)
*Junsheng Liu,Netanel Raviv*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文提出面向 torn paper channel 的局部对齐编码方案，可利用更短碎片中的信息，相比既有 interleaved-pilot 方法提高可达速率，并在带丢失碎片的推广模型中逼近容量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: torn paper channel 中码字被随机撕裂成无序碎片，解码关键在于全局对齐，即确定每个碎片原始位置。已有方案依赖全局统计，需要较长碎片，短碎片常被当作擦除，导致速率显著低于容量，因此需要能利用短碎片的新对齐方法。

Method: 作者提出改进编码方案，引入 local alignment。该方法仅利用每个碎片内部的局部信息识别全局对齐比特，从而确定比以往方法更短的碎片位置。并将分析扩展到 TPC-LP 模型，考虑长度相关的碎片删除概率，特别是删除低于对数长度阈值的碎片、对更长碎片允许任意长度相关删除概率的一类信道。

Result: 局部对齐使解码器能够从更大比例的信道输出碎片中提取信息，带来可证明的速率提升。在 TPC-LP 的指定信道类中，当长度阈值增大时，该策略可达到与容量仅相差任意小加性间隙的速率。

Conclusion: 论文表明，依赖局部信息的碎片对齐可显著缓解传统全局统计对齐对碎片长度的限制，提高 torn paper channel 的信息利用率和可达速率，并在含长度相关丢失的推广模型中具有近容量性能。

Abstract: In the torn paper channel, a transmitted codeword is broken at random locations into fragments that arrive at the decoder in an unordered manner. A central theoretical challenge within this model is global alignment -- the task of determining each fragment's original position -- in order to faithfully reconstruct the entire codeword. Prior work by Shomorony and Vahid introduced an interleaved-pilot scheme that successfully achieved a vanishing error probability. However, their alignment strategy relies heavily on global statistics, requiring fragments to exceed a minimum length and effectively discarding many shorter ones as erasures, which results in rates significantly below capacity. To address this gap, we propose an improved coding scheme that achieves a provable rate increase through a novel approach we call \textit{local alignment}. This approach identifies global alignment bits within each fragment using only local information, allowing the decoder to determine the positions of fragments that are shorter than those used in previous work. Consequently, the decoder can extract information from a much larger fraction of the channel output than in previous work, yielding significantly higher rates. Furthermore, we extend our analysis to torn paper coding with lost pieces (TPC-LP), a generalized model that accounts for length-dependent fragment deletion. For a class of TPC-LP channels that delete all fragments below a logarithmic length threshold while allowing arbitrary length-dependent deletion probabilities for longer fragments, we show that the proposed local alignment strategy achieves an arbitrarily small additive gap to capacity as the threshold increases.

</details>


### [126] [The Closure of LCD-to-GI Reductions via Generalized Inner Products](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23120)
*Keita Ishizuka*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究线性码置换等价问题中基于正交投影子的图同构归约方法，证明其可推广到双线性型 M=aI+bJ，并刻画其适用边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 既有结果表明，对线性互补对偶（LCD）码，PEP 可通过正交投影子归约到图同构问题，但该方法仅覆盖平凡 hull 的情形。本文旨在厘清该投影方法能否扩展、扩展到何种程度，以及其理论极限。

Method: 作者分析一般非退化对称双线性型下的正交投影构造，证明仅 M=aI+bJ 形式可产生有效归约；进一步给出码可归约的充要条件，并用二次型上的特征和推导精确枚举公式，同时设计多项式时间归约算法。

Result: 结果表明，一个码可归约当且仅当其 hull 维数至多为 1，并满足关于 hull 向量的显式条件；在特征 2 情形下，只有 LCD 码可归约。由此证明除 M=aI+bJ 外没有其他非退化对称型能支持该方法。

Conclusion: 本文完整刻画了正交投影子归约方法的适用范围，说明该方法在理论上已经闭合，并为相关可归约线性码的计数和算法实现提供了严格基础。

Abstract: The Permutation Equivalence Problem (PEP) for linear codes is a fundamental problem in coding theory and cryptography. A recent reduction shows that PEP for Linear Complementary Dual (LCD) codes reduces to Graph Isomorphism (GI) via orthogonal projectors, but is restricted to codes with trivial hull. We prove that this approach extends to bilinear forms $M = aI + bJ$, and that no other nondegenerate symmetric form yields a valid reduction. A code is reducible if and only if its hull dimension is at most $1$ with an explicit condition on the hull vector; in characteristic $2$, only LCD codes are reducible. This establishes the closure of the orthogonal projector method. We derive exact enumeration formulas via character sums over quadratic forms and provide a polynomial-time reduction algorithm.

</details>


### [127] [On APN Exponents and the Differential and Boomerang Properties of Binomials in Characteristic 3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23224)
*Namhun Koo,Soonhak Kwon,Minwoo Ko,Byunguk Kim*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究有限域 F_{3^n} 上形如 F_r(x)=x^r(1+χ(x)) 的二项式，系统刻画若干在特征 3 下具有极低 boomerang uniformity（0 或 1）的函数类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明此类二项式可能具有很低的 boomerang uniformity；在特征 3 中，达到 0 或 1 的情形似乎更常见，但缺乏系统分类与严格证明。

Method: 作者首先系统分析特征 3 下的 APN 幂函数，给出 Zha–Wang 构造所得 APN 指数的显式参数化，并用 n≤13 的数值实验验证其覆盖若干已知或零散实例；随后基于该分类构造并证明低 boomerang uniformity 的二项式类，并通过字符和计算完全确定特定指数情形的 boomerang 谱。

Result: 论文证明了两类由 APN 构造相关指数及 r=2·3^{(n-1)/2}+1 导出的二项式是 locally-PN 且 boomerang uniformity 为 0；还证明 r=3^n−3 时，当 n≥5 为奇数，F_r 为 locally-APN 且 boomerang uniformity 为 1，并完全给出其 boomerang spectrum。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展并统一了特征 3 中二项式密码性质的已有结果，给出了多个具有最小或近最小 boomerang uniformity 的函数族的系统性刻画。

Abstract: Recent studies on binomials of the form $F_r(x) = x^r(1 + χ(x))$ over $\mathbb{F}_{p^n}$ have shown that these functions can exhibit very low boomerang uniformity. In this paper, we focus on the specific behavior of such binomials in characteristic $3$, where instances of extremely low boomerang uniformity-namely $0$ or $1$-seem to arise more frequently than in other characteristics. First, we provide a systematic analysis of Almost Perfect Nonlinear (APN) power functions in characteristic $3$. We present an explicit parametrization of APN exponents arising from the construction of Zha and Wang and demonstrate through numerical results for $n \le 13$ that this generalized framework accounts for several previously known and sporadic APN instances. Building on this classification, we identify and rigorously prove two classes of binomials $F_r$ that are locally-PN and possess the minimum possible boomerang uniformity of $0$. These classes involve exponents derived from the aforementioned APN construction and the differentially 4-uniform exponent $r = 2 \cdot 3^{\frac{n-1}{2}} + 1$. Furthermore, we analyze the binomial $F_r$ with $r = 3^n - 3$, proving that it is locally-APN with boomerang uniformity $1$ when $n\ge 5$ is odd, and completely determine its boomerang spectrum through the evaluation of character sums. Our results clarify and extend existing studies on the cryptographic properties of binomials, providing a systematic characterization of several classes of binomials with very low boomerang uniformity in characteristic $3$.

</details>


### [128] [A Posterior MWPM Decoding Boosts the XYZ Planar Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23236)
*Zhiwei Wang,Liqi Wang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文提出XYZ planar code，并将MWPM解码扩展为pMWPM，以在偏置噪声下提升表面码解码性能且几乎不增加复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统表面码常用MWPM解码器，但在偏置噪声条件下性能显著下降；因此需要一种能适应不同噪声偏置、保持较高阈值并降低逻辑错误率的编码与解码方案。

Method: 作者引入改进型表面码——XYZ planar code，并将最小权完美匹配解码器扩展为posterior MWPM（pMWPM）。该方法利用后验信息改进匹配权重或解码决策，同时保持与原MWPM接近的解码复杂度，并可推广到其他改进表面码结构。

Result: XYZ planar code在几乎所有偏置条件下相比传统planar code具有更高且更稳定的阈值，并显著降低逻辑错误率。无限偏置情况下，其阈值相对表面码提升约36%；在η=1时阈值约为15.5%，在η=100时约为14.2%。

Conclusion: XYZ planar code结合pMWPM是一种在偏置噪声下更鲁棒的量子纠错方案，能在不明显增加解码复杂度的前提下提升阈值和逻辑性能；pMWPM还具备推广到其他修改型表面码及更复杂算符配置的潜力。

Abstract: The minimum-weight perfect matching (MWPM) decoder is a standard decoding strategy for surface codes, but its performance degrades considerably under biased noise. In this paper, a modified surface code, termed the XYZ planar code, is introduced, and the MWPM decoder is extended to posterior MWPM (pMWPM) with almost no increase in decoding complexity. The XYZ planar code exhibits higher and more stable thresholds than the planar code under almost all bias conditions, while also achieving significantly lower logical error rates. Specifically, in the infinite-bias case, the threshold of the XYZ planar code is improved by about \(36\%\) compared to that of the surface code, and it maintains comparable or higher thresholds under other biases -- for example, the threshold reaches approximately \(15.5\%\) at bias \(η= 1\) and \(14.2\%\) at \(η= 100\). Furthermore, pMWPM can be adapted to a wide range of modified surface codes, and the results presented in this work also indicate its excellent potential in other scenarios, such as configurations in which \(Y\) operators involve a larger number of data qubits.

</details>


### [129] [MISO Downlink with Fluid Antenna Multiple Access](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23260)
*Anastasios Papazafeiropoulos*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文建立了FAMA多用户MISO下行系统的统一解析框架，刻画MRT/ZF预编码下端口SIR分布、跨端口相关性与中断概率界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FAMA通过在多个紧密间隔端口间快速切换并选择最强接收信号来获得微尺度空间分集，但在存在空间相关与线性预编码的多用户下行系统中，其性能规律尚缺乏系统理解。

Method: 针对MISO下行FAMA用户，分别分析MRT与ZF预编码；证明单端口SIR服从参数为(M_eff,L)的Beta-prime分布，其中MRT下M_eff=M，ZF下M_eff=M-U+1；推导有限和形式的CDF，建立跨端口SIR相关性解析模型，并给出严格的中断概率上下界及渐近分析。

Result: 数值结果验证了SIR分布、相关模型和中断概率界的准确性；界在完全相关和独立端口极限下变为精确；当基站空间自由度充足时，MRT相比ZF表现出更弱的端口相关性和更大的选择增益。

Conclusion: 该框架揭示了FAMA系统在不同预编码下的分集阶数、尾部行为和端口选择收益，并为实际系统中的端口配置与预编码选择提供了明确指导。

Abstract: Fluid antenna multiple access (FAMA) enables each user to rapidly switch among several closely spaced ports and select the strongest received signal. Although this mechanism offers micro-scale spatial diversity, its behavior in multiuser downlink systems with spatial correlation and linear precoding is not well understood. This paper develops a unified analytical framework for the multiple-input single-output (MISO) downlink with FAMA users served via maximum ratio transmission (MRT) or zero-forcing (ZF). We show that the per-port signal-to-interference ratio
  (SIR) follows a Beta-prime distribution with parameters
  \((M_{\mathrm{eff}},L)\), where \(M_{\mathrm{eff}}=M\) under MRT and
  \(M_{\mathrm{eff}}=M-U+1\) under ZF, and derive closed-form finite-sum cumulative distribution functions (CDFs) for both cases. We further provide the first analytical characterization of cross-port SIR correlation. \textcolor{black}{Furthermore, we derive rigorous outage probability bounds that tightly bracket the exact performance and become exact in the limiting cases of fully correlated and independent ports.} Asymptotic analyses reveal the fundamental diversity orders and tail behavior for each precoder. Numerical results confirm the accuracy of the SIR distributions, correlation model, and outage bounds, and show that MRT achieves weaker port correlation and larger selection gains than ZF when the base station (BS) has ample spatial degrees of freedom. The framework offers explicit guidelines for port configuration and precoder selection in practical FAMA systems.

*Yanli Wang,Yanxin Chen,Tongjiang Yan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: This paper contributes to maximum distance separable (MDS) and near MDS (NMDS) properties of the extended generalized twisted Reed-Solomon (TGRS) codes. Secondly, the necessary and sufficient conditions for these codes to be MDS or almost MDS (AMDS) codes are derived. Then, by analyzing the AMDS properties of their dual codes, the necessary and sufffcient conditions for them to be NMDS codes are established. Furthermore, some examples are given to verify the main results. Finally, we determine the non-generalized Reed-Solomon (non-GRS) characteristics of them via the Schur product method.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统通信系统通常对所有消息提供均匀保护，主要追求降低误码率和提高传输速率；但在意图导向应用中，不同消息具有不同语义价值和重要性，因此需要按消息重要性提供不同可靠性保障。

Method: 论文采用分层码本构造方法，不再为码字附加显式保护标签，而是直接设计码本的汉明距离结构：为高重要性消息组分配更大的组内最小距离，并设置合适的组间距离约束，从而兼顾差错纠正能力与接收端重要性级别识别。

Abstract: Conventional communication systems are mainly designed to reduce error rates and increase transmission rates, and therefore usually provide uniform protection to all transmitted messages. However, in intent-oriented applications, different messages may have different semantic meanings and importance levels, requiring different levels of reliability. This paper proposes a layered construction of message-level unequal error protection (UEP) codes for short-blocklength communication. Instead of appending an explicit protection tag to each codeword, the proposed method embeds the protection structure directly into the Hamming-distance structure of the codebook. By assigning larger minimum intra-level distances to higher-importance message groups and imposing suitable inter-level distance constraints, the proposed codebook provides differentiated error-correction capabilities while enabling reliable importance-level classification at the receiver. Theoretical conditions for correct group classification are derived, and simulations over AWGN and VLC-ISI channels show that the proposed scheme improves BER performance and group classification accuracy compared with a tag-based ECC baseline.

*Mohammad Reza Deylam Salehi*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出 Dijkstra-pruned INL（D-INL），通过保留以融合节点为根、容量感知的最短路径树来剪除非树边，在显著降低训练通信开销的同时基本保持分类精度。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法使用 Dijkstra 策略构建容量感知最短路径树并剪除非树链路；同时将本地路由或聚合建模为有限速率随机门控，门控速率定义为 R_g=I(Z;T)，并推导率失真泛化界来解释稀疏化、信息率与泛化性能之间的关系。

Conclusion: D-INL 表明基于最短路径树的拓扑剪枝可有效降低分布式神经训练通信成本，而有限速率正则化可进一步压缩潜在信息传输，且不会明显损害预测性能。

Abstract: In-network learning (INL) trains distributed neural modules by exchanging latent activations and backpropagated errors over a communication graph. This letter proposes Dijkstra-pruned INL (D-INL), which removes non-tree links by retaining a capacity-aware shortest-path tree rooted at the fusion node. To balance sparsity and predictive information, local routing (or aggregation) is modeled as a finite-rate stochastic gate with rate $R_g=I(Z; T)$. We derive a rate-distortion-generalization bound and validate the method on a reproducible distributed-classification experiment, where D-INL reduces training exchange by $70.4\%$ while preserving accuracy within the standard deviation of dense INL. Adding finite-rate regularization further reduces the estimated latent rate by $45.7\%$ relative to unregularized Dijkstra INL.

### [134] [Multi-User MIMO with Rotatable Antennas and IRS: Joint Antenna Boresight and IRS Orientation Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23683)
*Guoying Zhang,Qingqing Wu,Ziyuan Zheng,Qiaoyan Peng,Ailing Zheng,Yanze Zhu,Ying Gao,Wen Chen*

We formulate a sum-rate maximization problem by jointly optimizing the receive beamforming, IRS phase shifts, BS antenna boresights, and IRS panel orientation. To tackle the resulting highly coupled and non-convex problem, we first study a single-user case to reveal the structure of the dual-rotation gain, which is shown to be multiplicatively separable in the far field but coupled in the near field. For the general multi-user case, we develop an alternating optimization algorithm, where the receive beamforming is updated in closed form, the IRS phase shifts are optimized by an FP-assisted Riemannian conjugate gradient method, and the BS antenna boresights and IRS panel orientation are updated via projected gradient methods. Simulation results demonstrate the significant sum-rate gains achieved by the proposed coordinated rotation design over fixed-orientation and single-rotation benchmark schemes, and provide useful insights into near-field dual-rotation design.

### [135] [BOHM: Zero-Cost Hierarchical Attribution for Compound AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22866)
*Joss Armstrong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: BOHM是一种利用复合AI系统已有路由权重生成层级归因树的方法，可在无需评估组件子集、无需访问内部细节的情况下，以零边际成本提供多分辨率归因；它与SHAP回答不同问题，差异可作为诊断信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SHAP类归因方法需要在任意组件子集上评估系统，但第三方API、黑盒端点和智能体编排器往往无法支持这种评估，且实际路由常集中于少数工具，导致大量联盟不可评估。

Method: 提出BOHM：直接从系统维护的路由权重中抽取层级归因树。叶节点归因为根到叶路径上路由权重的乘积；第k层归因为深度k节点上的诱导分布，从而同时得到各层级的归因结果。

Result: 在18个LLM、3层层级、880个LiveCodeBench问题上，BOHM Kendall tau=0.928；SHAP tau=0.980但每个seed需要约9000倍联盟评估。在35个智能体实验单元中，路由集中于单一工具，BOHM与SHAP的一致性取决于驱动器首选工具是否为经验最优工具。在Census层级数据上，BOHM在各层恢复真实排序，tau最高0.722。

Conclusion: BOHM满足效率、单调性、对称性和弱抑制性质，但不满足Shapley加性。它不是SHAP的替代品，而是互补的层级归因原语，尤其适用于存在路由状态但难以进行联盟评估的复合AI系统。

Abstract: Compound AI systems route tasks through hierarchies of specialised components. Attribution is dominated by Shapley-based methods (SHAP), which decompose a coalition value function into per-component marginal contributions and require evaluation of the system on arbitrary component subsets. That requirement fails for third-party APIs, opaque endpoints, and agentic orchestrators that concentrate routing on a few tools, leaving most coalitions un-evaluable from the deployed orchestrator. We introduce BOHM, which extracts a hierarchical attribution tree directly from the routing weights such systems already maintain: leaf attribution is the path product of root-to-leaf routing weights; level-k attribution is the induced distribution over depth-k nodes. The method has zero marginal cost, requires no access to component internals, and provides multi-resolution attribution at every level simultaneously, which flat methods cannot offer at any evaluation budget. BOHM and SHAP answer different questions and converge when the deployed router routes near-optimally. On 18 LLMs in a 3-level hierarchy over 880 LiveCodeBench problems, BOHM yields Kendall tau=0.928; SHAP reaches tau=0.980 at 9,000x more coalition evaluations per seed. On a 5-driver, 7-benchmark agentic study (35 cells, complete coverage), drivers concentrate routing on a single tool (top-share median 0.65), and cell-level tau(BOHM,SHAP) is predicted by whether the driver's top pick is the empirically best tool (mean +0.22 vs ~+0.01). On a US Census hierarchy (475 leaves, 4 levels), BOHM recovers ground-truth rankings at every level (tau up to 0.722). BOHM satisfies efficiency, monotonicity, symmetry, and weak suppression but not Shapley's additivity. It is best understood as a complementary primitive: a multi-resolution decomposition computable wherever routing state exists, whose disagreement with Shapley is itself diagnostic.

</details>


### [136] [NeuroNL2LTL: A Neurosymbolic Framework for Natural Language Translation of Linear Temporal Logic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22874)
*Paapa Kwesi Quansah,Ernest Bonnah*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 NeuroNL2LTL：一种神经符号架构，将自然语言需求翻译为线性时序逻辑，并通过形式验证约束训练与运行时输出，以提升规格生成的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然语言到形式逻辑（如 LTL）的转换需要专业知识，限制了形式验证在安全关键系统开发中的应用；模板方法可靠但表达能力有限，纯神经方法流畅但缺乏正确性保证。

Method: 方法采用中间表示作为 NL 到 LTL 的桥梁，保证到 LTL 的映射在结构上保持一致；对生成规格进行可满足性与非平凡性检查；用最小编辑修复机制纠正近似错误；并将验证结果作为强化学习奖励，进行 verifier-in-the-loop 训练。

Result: 在覆盖航空航天、机器人、自动驾驶等 13 个领域、超过 20 万条需求的数据上，系统达到 28% 的语义等价率，并保证 86% 的输出通过可满足性验证；同时可从 LTL 生成面向领域专家的上下文解释。

Conclusion: 论文表明形式验证不仅可作为神经规格生成系统的运行时过滤器，也可作为训练目标，使神经工具的可靠性更多来自逻辑保证而非统计置信度。

Abstract: Effectively translating between natural language (NL) and formal logics like Linear Temporal Logic (LTL) requires expertise that limits formal verification's reach in safety-critical development. Template-based approaches sacrifice expressiveness for reliability; neural methods achieve fluency but provide no correctness guarantees. We present NeuroNL2LTL, a neurosymbolic architecture unifying learned translation with formal verification. NeuroNL2LTL routes translation through an intermediate representation whose mapping to LTL is structure-preserving by construction. Generated specifications undergo satisfiability and non-triviality checking; a minimal-edit repair mechanism corrects near-miss outputs before they reach downstream tools. The central innovation is verifier-in-the-loop training: verification outcomes serve as reward signals for reinforcement learning, producing neural components that optimize directly for formal correctness. On 200,000+ requirements spanning aerospace, robotics, autonomous vehicles, and ten additional domains, NeuroNL2LTL achieves 28\% semantic equivalence with reference specifications while ensuring 86\% of outputs are verified satisfiable. The system also generates contextually grounded explanations from LTL, enabling domain experts to validate specifications without specialized training. This work demonstrates that formal verification can function as both training objective and runtime filter for neural specification systems, allowing us to build neural-based tools whose reliability derives from logical guarantees rather than statistical confidence.

### [137] [RMA: an Agentic System for Research-Level Mathematical Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22875)
*Zelin Zhao,Bo Yuan,Jaemoo Choi,Yongxin Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 Research Math Agents（RMA），一个面向研究级数学问题自动推理的多智能体框架，在 First Proof 基准上优于强基线，解决了 10 个问题中的 8 个。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: RMA 将研究级证明求解分解为问题分析、文献检索与理解、公平比较、知识库构建和证明验证等模块，并由 initializer、proposer、verifier 智能体通过共享结构化记忆协调。系统采用多角色、多轮协作流程，迭代生成、修订并验证候选证明。

Result: 在由专家数学家贡献的 First Proof 基准（10 个研究级问题）上，RMA 相比 GPT-5.2R 和 Aletheia 等强基线表现更好，解决 8/10 个问题，并生成逻辑更可靠、可读性更强的证明。消融实验表明，性能提升来自结构化推理模块、迭代 refinement 与 verifier 反馈之间的交互，而非单一组件。

Conclusion: RMA 展示了多智能体、模块化与迭代验证机制在研究级数学自动推理中的有效性，为从竞赛级推理走向真实研究问题求解提供了有前景的框架。

Abstract: We present $\textbf{Research Math Agents (RMA)}$, an agentic framework for automated reasoning on research-level mathematical problems. Unlike prior studies centered on competition mathematics or formal theorem proving, RMA targets research-level mathematical problems that require long-horizon reasoning, literature grounding, and iterative proof refinement. RMA decomposes research-level proof solving into specialized modules for problem analysis, literature search and understanding, fair comparison, knowledge-bank construction, and proof verification, all coordinated by initializer, proposer, and verifier agents through a shared structured memory. Within this unified framework, these agents operate in a multi-role, multi-round workflow, collaboratively generating, refining, and verifying candidate proofs through iterative feedback. We evaluate RMA on the First Proof benchmark, which consists of ten research-level problems contributed by expert mathematicians across diverse domains. Through comprehensive expert evaluation, RMA outperforms strong baselines on the First Proof benchmark, including GPT-5.2R and Aletheia, solving eight out of ten research problems and producing more logically sound and readable proofs. Our comprehensive ablation studies further show that performance gains arise from the interaction of structured reasoning modules, iterative refinement, and verifier-based feedback, rather than any single component. Our solutions and implementations will be made publicly available upon acceptance.

### [138] [Energy per Successful Goal: Goal-Level Energy Accounting for Agentic AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22883)
*Deepak Panigrahy,Aakash Tyagi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 A-LEMS，将智能体系统能耗评测单位从“每次推理能耗”改为“每个成功目标能耗”（EpG），并用 OOI 衡量编排开销，发现智能体工作流总体能耗显著高于线性基线，但在部分工具增强任务中可更省能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 AI 能耗基准多按单次模型调用或单次训练运行计量，适用于传统单轮任务；但智能体系统完成一个用户目标往往包含多步编排、工具调用、重试和故障恢复，调用次数只是实现细节，无法真实反映完成目标的能耗。

Method: 提出跨层测量框架 A-LEMS：以 Energy per Successful Goal（EpG）聚合所有执行尝试、失败与重试的总工作流能耗，并按成功完成目标归一化；通过时间边界模型、五层观测管线将 RAPL 信号映射到工作流级能耗；制定绑定硬件与运行时配置的可复现实验协议；进一步定义 Orchestration Overhead Index（OOI）以隔离相同任务标准下相对于线性执行的编排能耗开销。

Result: 在五类推理任务和三类工具增强任务上，智能体工作流的平均每成功目标能耗为 888.1 J，线性基线为 205.3 J，前者约为后者的 4.33 倍。该开销主要由编排结构而非单纯推理计算导致。在工具增强任务中，OOI 可低于 1.0，说明智能体执行在某些情况下比线性方式更省能。

Conclusion: 每次推理能耗不足以评估智能体 AI 的真实能耗。EpG 和 OOI 为面向目标完成的能耗基准提供了更准确的计量基础，并揭示编排结构是智能体系统能耗成本的关键决定因素。

Abstract: Current AI energy benchmarks measure consumption at the granularity of a single model invocation or training run. For classical single-turn workloads this unit remains coherent. For agentic systems - where a single user goal may trigger multi-step orchestration, tool calls, retries, and failure-recovery cycles - the invocation count is an implementation artifact rather than a task property, and inference-level normalization misrepresents the energy cost of goal completion. We present A-LEMS (Agentic LLM Energy Measurement System), a cross-layer measurement framework that redefines the unit of AI energy accounting from energy per inference to Energy per Successful Goal (EpG). EpG aggregates total workflow energy across all execution attempts, including failures and retries, normalized by successfully completed goals. A-LEMS formalizes energy attribution through a temporal boundary model, a five-layer observation pipeline mapping RAPL signals to workflow-level energy, and a reproducibility protocol binding every measurement to hardware and runtime configuration. Building on EpG, we define the Orchestration Overhead Index (OOI), isolating the energy cost of orchestration relative to linear execution under identical task criteria.
  Across five reasoning and three tool-augmented task families, agentic workflows consume 4.33x higher mean energy per successful goal than linear baselines (888.1 J vs 205.3 J). This overhead is driven by orchestration structure, not inference compute. For tool-augmented tasks, OOI inverts below 1.0x: agentic execution is cheaper than linear, confirming the metric captures orchestration structure rather than a fixed upward bias.
  These findings establish that energy-per-inference is insufficient for agentic AI. EpG and OOI provide the measurement foundation for accurate benchmarking, where orchestration structure is the primary determinant of energy cost.

</details>

ImProver 2 combines a data-efficient expert-iteration pipeline with a scaffold that exposes formal structure alongside lightweight informal abstractions. Using ImProver 2, we train a 7B-parameter model that outperforms orders-of-magnitude larger models within the same model family, and is competitive with mid-tier frontier models across metrics.   <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 论文证明了该系统的可靠性、容矛盾性，以及在不含 mediative 连接词公式上相对于底层模糊逻辑的保守性；并通过自动制动传感器融合示例展示其在不完整、异质且轻度矛盾证据下的透明、保守和安全优先决策能力。

Abstract: Mediative Fuzzy Logic was conceived as a practical scheme for reconciling hesitant or conflicting assessments in fuzzy control and decision-making. However, its logical and semantic foundations remain underdeveloped, especially beyond operational type-1 settings. This article develops a unified account of the type-1 core together with interval type-2, granular type-3, and quantum extensions. We characterize the mediative operator as a convex aggregation controlled by hesitation and contradiction, model mediative truth values as independent truth-falsity pairs in a continuous bilattice-like structure, and introduce a propositional system extending a standard t-norm-based fuzzy logic with a mediative connective. We establish soundness, paraconsistency, and conservativity over the underlying fuzzy base for formulas without mediation, and formulate coherent semantic extensions to interval type-2 truth values, granule-indexed local evaluations, and effects and density operators on Hilbert spaces. An autonomous-braking sensor-fusion example illustrates how the framework supports transparent, conservative, and safety-first decisions under incomplete, heterogeneous, and mildly contradictory evidence. Under suitable assumptions, the higher-level formulations reduce to the type-1 case, clarifying coherence across levels and reliably supporting future work in intelligent decision systems.

### [141] [EVE-Agent: Evidence-Verifiable Self-Evolving Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22905)
*Yamato Arai,Yuma Ichikawa*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 EVE-Agent，使自演化搜索智能体在生成训练样例时必须附带可验证的来源证据片段，并用证据对答案准确性的边际提升作为奖励信号，从而提升训练数据可信度与可审计性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无数据自演化搜索智能体可自行生成问题、答案并基于反馈改进，但若缺乏可验证证据，模型可能奖励流畅却无依据的样例，导致自生成课程不透明且不可靠。因此，作者认为证据可验证性是可信自演化的前提。

Method: 提出 Evidence-Verifiable Self-Evolving Agent（EVE-Agent），在 proposer--solver 框架中要求 proposer 同时生成问题、答案和逐字引用的证据片段；再由证据验证器根据“提供该证据后答案准确性的边际增益”对证据进行奖励。该方法不依赖人工标注、标准答案或外部注释，也不改变骨干模型、检索器、搜索工具和优化框架。

Result: 实验表明，相比既有自演化搜索智能体，EVE-Agent 在证据支撑的正确性方面有显著提升。

Conclusion: EVE-Agent 将自生成训练样例转化为带有可检查来源证据的可审计课程，使自演化过程更可信，减少无依据但表面合理样例带来的训练风险。

Abstract: Self-evolving agents should not train on examples they cannot justify. Data-free self-evolving search agents offer a scalable route to systems that generate their own questions, answer them, and improve from their own feedback without human annotations. Yet, without verifiable evidence, this loop can reward fluent but unsupported examples, turning the self-generated curriculum into an opaque and potentially unreliable training signal. We argue that evidence verifiability is a prerequisite for trustworthy self-evolution in search agents: each generated instance should include not only an answer but also a source-grounded span whose contribution to that answer can be measured. We introduce EVE-Agent, an Evidence-Verifiable Self-Evolving Agent that operationalizes this principle through a modification to the proposer--solver framework. The proposer generates a question, an answer, and a verbatim evidence span. An evidence verifier then rewards the span according to the marginal accuracy gain when the evidence is provided. This produces a training signal that favors evidence that genuinely helps answer the question, without requiring oracle answers, human labels, or external annotations. EVE-Agent leaves the backbone model, retriever, search tool, and optimization framework unchanged. Experiments show that EVE-Agent substantially improves evidence-grounded correctness over prior self-evolving search agents. The resulting curriculum is not merely self-generated but auditable by construction: each training example carries an inspectable source span that explains why it should be trusted.

### [142] [The Deterministic Horizon: Impossibility Results as Design Specifications for Trustworthy AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23024)
*Dongxin Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文/学位论文主张将计算与学习中的不可能性结果转化为可信AI系统设计规则，核心贡献是提出可部署前计算的“确定性地平线”，刻画Transformer在超过临界推理深度后的架构性准确率上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型已被用于软件、法律、临床文本等高风险任务，但其能力受图灵不可判定性、Arrow定理、No Free Lunch等基础限制约束。作者希望把这些理论边界从抽象负结果转化为可操作的系统规格、风险成本与设计原则，以服务可信AI。

Method: 论文以不可能性—规格化方法为主线：基于层数与嵌入宽度推导Transformer推理深度的架构性上限；用残差流容量不变量解释机制，并通过信息论转换得到超指数准确率衰减；同时扩展到电路复杂度、偏好学习、检索流水线、拍卖机制与神经推理零知识验证等场景，形成多项可计算边界和设计规则。

Result: 在12种Transformer架构上，确定性地平线被测得约为19到31；超过该深度后，无论适配器秩、样本量或损失函数如何增加，训练均难以突破该上限；针对最优长度推理轨迹的微调仅恢复不到4个百分点。论文还给出模指数运算相对于常深度素模电路的无条件复杂度下界，并报告神经推理零知识验证中每个非线性激活约110到190倍开销。

Conclusion: 论文结论是：AI的基础限制不只是能力边界，也可作为工程设计规则。通过为每个限制配套可计算边界、量化违规成本与建设性设计原则，可形成面向可信AI的系统化研究方案；但部分规格组合仍为开放问题。

Abstract: Large language models now write software, draft legal documents, and produce clinical notes, yet fundamental limits, from Turing and Arrow to the No Free Lunch theorems, shape what computation can do. This thesis turns such impossibility results from curiosities into design rules. Its flagship result proves an accuracy ceiling set by architecture alone: past a critical reasoning depth, no amount of training moves it, at any adapter rank, sample size, or loss function. Computable before deployment from layer count and embedding width, this Deterministic Horizon is measured between nineteen and thirty-one across twelve transformer architectures, and fine-tuning on optimal-length traces recovers under four percentage points. The mechanism is a capacity invariant of the residual stream, and an information-theoretic conversion yields super-exponential accuracy decay past the horizon. An unconditional circuit-complexity lower bound for modular exponentiation against constant-depth prime-modulus circuits complements this result. The same argument recasts across subfields: preference learning under any misspecified model jumps discontinuously in sample complexity; multi-stage retrieval pipelines require at least as many independent metrics as stages; standard truthful auctions fail for agents with prompt-dependent valuations; and zero-knowledge verification of neural inference pays a measured overhead of one hundred ten to one hundred ninety times per non-linear activation. Together these form a catalogue of sixteen specifications, each pairing a computable boundary, a quantified violation cost, and a constructive design rule: two compositions are proved, one pairing is an honest obstruction, and four remain open. The impossibility-specification methodology is offered for the generative research programme that trustworthy AI may need. Every fundamental limit of AI is also a design rule.

### [143] [PathCal: State-Aware Reflection-Marker Calibration for Efficient Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23074)
*Lingyu Jiang,Zirui Li,Shuo Xing,Peiran Li,Tsubasa Takahashi,Dengzhe Hou,Zhengzhong Tu,Kazunori Yamada,Fangzhou Lin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 PathCal：一种无需训练的解码控制器，通过区分不同反思标记类型并仅在局部不确定状态介入，以减少长链式推理生成长度，同时保持或提升准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理语言模型在推理时会生成长形式 CoT，其中包含“wait”“but”“alternatively”等反思标记。已有测试时控制方法通常将这些标记视为同一粗粒度类别，忽略了不同标记在功能角色和影响时机上的差异，因此难以实现更精细、更高效的推理路径控制。

Method: 作者先进行按类型抑制和固定前缀干预实验，分析不同反思标记类别对准确率与生成长度的影响，以及其作用发生的关键阶段。基于发现，提出 PathCal：在每个解码步利用反思标记分布估计当前推理轨迹与竞争分支之间的局部竞争程度；当竞争分支证据过强时，对相关标记 logits 进行软性重平衡，从而校准推理路径。该方法无需训练、无需外部验证器，也不依赖额外采样。

Result: 在六个推理基准上的实验表明，PathCal 能在提升或保持准确率的同时减少生成长度，相比常规测试时控制方法实现更优的效率—性能折中。

Conclusion: 反思标记并非同质信号，不同类型在推理过程中的功能和作用时机存在显著差异。利用这些差异进行局部、不确定性驱动的软干预，可以更有效地控制 LRMs 的推理路径，降低冗余生成并保持推理质量。

Abstract: The emergence of Large Reasoning Language Models (LRMs) has paved the way for tackling complex reasoning tasks through test-time scaling by generating long-form Chain-of-Thought (CoT) trajectories during inference. Meanwhile, these trajectories often contain explicit reflection markers such as ``wait'', ``but'', and ``alternatively'', signaling hesitation, revision, and the consideration of alternative explorations, respectively. Recent studies on test-time control leverage such markers as lightweight handles for steering reasoning, typically treating them as a single coarse-grained category rather than distinguishing their distinct functional roles. In this paper, we conduct type-wise suppression and fixed-prefix intervention, revealing that reflection markers differ not only in their functional roles but also in when they exert the greatest influence. Specifically, different marker classes affect accuracy and generation length in distinct ways, and marker choices are most consequential before the model settles into a stable reasoning trajectory. Motivated by these findings, we introduce PathCal, a novel training-free decoding controller that calibrates reasoning paths by distinguishing marker types and intervening only at locally uncertain states. At each decoding step, PathCal utilizes the distribution over reflection-markers to estimate local competition between maintaining the current reasoning trajectory and initiating a competing branch, and softly rebalances marker logits when competing-branch evidence becomes excessive. Experiments across six reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PathCal achieves a better efficiency--performance trade-off, improving or preserving accuracy while reducing generation length, without relying on external verifiers or additional sampling.

</details>


### [144] [Inductive Deductive Synthesis: Enabling AI to Generate Formally Verified Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23109)
*Shubham Agarwal,Alexander Krentsel,Shu Liu,Mert Cemri,Audrey Cheng,Rui Meng,Tomas Pfister,Chun-Liang Li,Sylvia Ratnasamy,Aditya Parameswaran,Matei Zaharia,Ion Stoica,Mohsen Lesani*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 Inductive Deductive Synthesis（IDS），一种面向分布式系统形式化验证代码生成的智能体式 LLM 方法，能联合合成实现与证明，并在实验中显著优于现有编码智能体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 AI 编码智能体擅长生成、测试和迭代代码，但对需要全覆盖形式化保证的任务能力不足；分布式系统需要在所有事件交错下保证一致性等性质，而机械化形式化验证通常需要专家投入数月至数年。

Method: 提出 IDS：联合且增量地合成系统实现与形式化证明；从失败尝试中学习，系统性探索更有希望的策略；并将性能反馈纳入同一优化循环。该方法被实现为 agentic LLM system。

Result: 在 7 个分布式键值存储规格上，SOTA 编码智能体仅完成 2/7，而 IDS 完成 7/7；平均每个规格约 6.8 小时、成本 106 美元；相比专家工作约快 200 倍，比 SOTA 智能体便宜 17%；性能优化后实现最高比已发表验证系统快 3 倍。

Conclusion: IDS 展示了 LLM 智能体在形式化验证驱动的软件合成中可显著提升成功率、效率和性能，尤其适用于需要强正确性保证的分布式系统。

Abstract: AI agents increasingly excel at generating, testing, and refining code. However, they fall short on tasks requiring formal guarantees of full coverage that testing alone cannot provide. Distributed systems are a prime example: properties such as consistency between reads and writes must hold under every possible interleaving of events. Mechanized formal verification can guarantee such correctness, but typically demands months to years of expert effort. As evidence, even SOTA coding agents (Codex with GPT-5.4 and Claude Code with Opus 4.6) succeed on only 2/7 distributed key-value-store specifications. In this paper, we present the first effective approach to addressing this gap, Inductive Deductive Synthesis (IDS), which jointly and incrementally synthesizes implementation and proof, and learns from failed attempts to systematically try promising strategies. Built as an agentic LLM system, IDS achieves 7/7 in about 6.8 hours and $106 per spec on average, roughly 200x faster than expert effort and 17% cheaper than SOTA agents. IDS further incorporates performance feedback into the same loop, yielding implementations up to 3x faster than published verified systems.

</details>


### [145] [Redrawing the AI Map: A Theory of Accountability Boundaries in Agentic Ecosystems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23179)
*Muhammad Zia Hydari,Farooq Muzaffar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种关于智能体 AI 生态中“问责边界”如何放置的能力层级理论，解释技术模块化何时会带来组织解聚，何时会因问责需求而保持整合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体 AI 编排器降低了跨组织组合信息系统能力的接口与装配成本，似乎会推动模块化和组织解聚；但许多 AI 输出仍需要证据、审查、签署与责任归属，因此技术边界变得模块化并不必然意味着问责边界也会外移。

Method: 论文进行概念理论构建，整合数字创新、交易成本、互补资产、数字平台治理和信息系统控制等视角，提出“问责资产”“规则债务”等概念，并形成七个理论命题；同时通过文档处理、法律服务、审计、临床决策支持和采购等结构化场景说明边界逻辑。

Result: 论文识别出三类边界策略：组件式、整合式和双轨式；指出验证成本与责任可转移性决定执行边界和问责边界能否同步移动；并阐明编排器意图捕获、问责资产、可占有性和边界错配如何影响价值获取与规则债务。

Conclusion: 数字模块化只有在问责资产可外部化、验证成本较低且责任可清晰转移时，才更可能推动组织解聚；若 AI 输出高度依赖审查、合法性、可审计性和明确责任主体，则组织仍需维持整合型问责边界。

Abstract: Agentic AI orchestrators reduce the interface and assembly costs of composing information systems capabilities across organizational boundaries, seemingly accelerating modularization and organizational disaggregation. Yet AI-enabled capabilities whose outputs require evidence, review, signoff, or assignable responsibility may retain integrated accountability boundaries even when their technical interfaces become modular. We develop a capability-level theory of accountability-boundary placement in agentic ecosystems. We introduce accountability assets: complementary assets that make AI-supported outputs legitimate, auditable, reviewable, and assignable to a responsible party. We argue that verification cost and responsibility transferability determine whether the execution and accountability boundaries can move together. The theory identifies three boundary strategies: component, integrated, and dual-track. It also introduces rule debt, the governance burden that accrues when organizational decision rules migrate from formal information systems into ungoverned agentic execution environments. Integrating digital innovation, transaction cost, complementary-assets, digital platform governance, and IS control perspectives, we develop seven propositions linking agentic assembly-cost reductions, accountability assets, appropriability, orchestrator intent capture, and boundary misconfiguration to boundary strategy, value appropriation, and rule debt. The theory explains when digital modularization extends to organizational disaggregation and when accountability keeps capabilities integrated. Structured illustrations across document processing, legal services, audit, clinical decision support, and procurement discipline the boundary logic.

### [146] [AutoResearch AI: Towards AI-Powered Research Automation for Scientific Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23204)
*Guiyao Tie,Jiawen Shi,Dingjie Song,Yixiao Huang,Ziji Sheng,Xueyang Zhou,Daizong Liu,Pan Zhou,Yongchao Chen,Ran Xu,Lifang He,Qingsong Wen,Manling Li,Cong Lu,Shuai Li,Pengtao Xie,Yixuan Yuan,Rui Meng,Lei Xing,Lichao Sun,Caiming Xiong,Philip S. Yu,Jianfeng Gao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文综述了从任务级“AI for Science”向工作流级科研自动化（AutoResearch）演进的趋势，提出分类框架、关键条件与评价维度，并指出当前系统仍受可验证性、溯源、复现性和问责边界限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI科研系统正在从单点辅助扩展到覆盖文献 grounding、假设生成、实验执行、验证、报告与修订的长周期流程，但现有系统在自主性、领域适用性、执行环境、验证机制与人类监督方式上高度碎片化，缺乏统一概念框架和评价标准。

Result: 论文归纳出科研工作流中控制权、证据、执行、验证与问责的重新分配方式，提出五个评价维度：新颖性、有效性、影响力、可靠性和溯源性；并指出 AutoResearch 的可信自主性强烈依赖领域条件。

Conclusion: AutoResearch 在结构化、可执行、快速验证的场景中更具可行性，但在具身实验、长期反馈、异构任务、伦理约束或需要制度性问责的科研环境中仍难以实现稳健自主；未来关键在于证据保存、可复现验证、弱方向拒绝、过程溯源和可问责闭环。

Abstract: Scientific research is being reshaped by AI systems that move beyond isolated assistance toward longer-horizon workflows spanning literature grounding, hypothesis generation, experimentation, validation, reporting, and revision. This shift marks a transition from task-level AI for science to workflow-level research automation. Yet current systems remain fragmented, differing in autonomy, domain scope, execution environment, validation mechanism, and human oversight, while still struggling with evidence preservation, reproducibility, weak-direction rejection, provenance tracking, cross-domain robustness, and accountable scientific closure. This survey examines these developments through AutoResearch, defined as the developmental spectrum of AI-powered scientific workflow automation. Within it, Vibe Research denotes the human-steered region of prompt-based assistance and human-verified execution, whereas emerging AI-led systems coordinate larger portions of the discovery loop without achieving robust autonomy. We analyze how research systems redistribute control, evidence, execution, validation, and accountability across workflows and organize the field around five workflow conditions: literature and research grounding; hypothesis formation and planning; experimentation and tool use; feedback, validation, and review; and reporting and knowledge communication. We further synthesize AI scientist systems, mixed-initiative co-research frameworks, benchmarks, domain deployments, and open-source infrastructures. Finally, we propose five evaluation dimensions--novelty, validity, impact, reliability, and provenance--and show that AutoResearch autonomy is domain-conditioned, being more credible in structured, executable, and rapidly verifiable settings but limited in embodied, delayed, heterogeneous, ethical, or institutionally accountable contexts.

### [147] [GENSTRAT: Toward a Science of Strategic Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23238)
*Vartan Shadarevian,Kia Ghods,Alex Kenich,Anany Kotawala*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 GENSTRAT：通过程序生成的双人零和不完全信息纸牌博弈来持续评估大语言模型的战略推理能力，并用能力画像与“锯齿性”指标揭示总体排名之外的部署风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有战略推理基准多依赖固定经典博弈，容易随模型进步而饱和，也可能受到数据污染影响；更重要的是，它们难以将基准表现可靠推广到真实部署中复杂、多样、非规范化的市场、拍卖和竞价等战略环境。

Method: 作者构建 GENSTRAT，程序化生成一类双人零和不完全信息纸牌游戏，可按需生成新游戏以保持评测常新并降低污染风险。同时提出能力画像方法，从状态空间、时间深度、信息敏感性、对手建模、风险、脆弱性六个维度分解模型能力；并设计“锯齿性”度量，用于检测模型在战略相似游戏之间表现是否出现不可预测跳变。实验从 2,000 个生成游戏池中抽取 50 个基准游戏，对 9 个前沿及开源权重 LLM 进行超过 36,000 场头对头锦标赛评估。

Result: 较新的前沿模型平均得分更高。但总体强度接近的模型在能力画像上呈现明显差异；排行榜前三中，gpt-5 和 claude 相比 gemini-3.1-pro 表现出更强的局部波动性，尽管它们整体实力接近。

Conclusion: GENSTRAT 通过生成式环境、能力画像和锯齿性指标，提供了比单一排行榜更具部署相关性的诊断框架，可揭示模型在相似战略环境中的稳定性、能力结构和潜在风险。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as economic agents in marketplaces, auctions, and bidding settings. Anticipating their behavior in any specific deployment is hard. Existing strategic-reasoning benchmarks evaluate models on fixed canonical games. These benchmarks may saturate as the frontier improves, and they do not allow evaluators to generalize with confidence from benchmark performance to the varied and messy strategic environments that actual deployments involve. We introduce GENSTRAT, which uses procedurally generated strategic environments to address these challenges. Concretely, we generate a distribution of two-player zero-sum imperfect-information card games. The generator can draw fresh games on demand, allowing for evergreen evaluation and resistance to contamination. We pair the game distribution with a capability-profile methodology that decomposes model competence across six axes (state space, temporal depth, information sensitivity, opponent modeling, risk, and brittleness). We also introduce a jaggedness measure of within-distribution smoothness that detects when a model's advantage jumps unpredictably between strategically similar games. We sample 50 benchmark games from a 2,000-game generated pool and evaluate nine frontier and open-weight LLMs in a head-to-head tournament with over 36,000 matches. Newer frontier-tier models score higher on average. Beyond that average, models with near-identical overall strength show qualitatively different capability profiles, and two of the top three leaderboard models (gpt-5 and claude) are noticeably more locally volatile than the third (gemini-3.1-pro), despite being close in overall strength. Together, the capability profile and the jaggedness measure give a deployment-relevant diagnostic that the overall ranking alone cannot provide.

*Yining Hua,Hongbin Na,Cyrus Ayubcha,Levi Lian*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种三步法，用于明确AI知识工作基准测试分数能够支持何种真实工作能力主张：定义工作活动、说明测试情境、评价合适的工作产物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM agent与知识工作评测多沿用传统NLP任务逻辑，导致高分并不必然代表系统能在真实部署环境中完成知识工作；因此需要更清晰地连接基准任务、测试条件、评分对象与现实工作主张。

Method: 作者基于工作研究文献，强调知识工作由角色职责、本地材料与工具、以及可被下游流程继续使用的产物组织起来；据此提出基准设计与报告指南，并从O*NET职业任务数据库归纳出18类工作活动，用于命名和区分被评估的工作能力；同时分析GDPval、OfficeQA Pro和APEX-SWE三个案例。

Result: 案例分析表明，不同基准的任务设计、测试设置和评分对象会显著影响其分数所能支持的最强工作能力主张，并暴露出基准任务、测试情境、评分产物与更广泛工作声明之间的缺口。

Abstract: The development of LLM agents has led to a growing body of work on knowledge-work AI, including coding, research, and healthcare. However, current knowledge-work evaluation and benchmark design still largely follow the logic of traditional NLP tasks. As a result, higher benchmark performance does not reliably show that a system can carry out knowledge work in real-world deployment settings. This paper contributes a three-step approach for making explicit how benchmarked tasks represent the work claims attached to their scores: defining the work activity under evaluation, specifying the tested setting, and scoring the appropriate work product. We review work studies showing that knowledge work is organized through roles and responsibilities, local materials and tools, and artifacts that must remain usable in downstream workflows. We then translate these concerns into benchmark design and reporting guidance, covering how tasks should be mapped to work activities, how tested settings should specify materials, tools, roles, and constraints, and how scoring should focus on the work product left by the system. To name the work activity being evaluated and distinguish it from common benchmark tasks, we derive an inventory of 18 work activities from the O{*}NET occupational task database. We demonstrate the approach through three benchmark case analyses: GDPval, a non-code occupational deliverable benchmark; OfficeQA Pro, a grounded document-analysis benchmark scored by final answers; and APEX-SWE, a software-engineering benchmark with executable scored products. These cases show how benchmark design choices shape the strongest work claim a score can support, and where gaps arise between the benchmarked task, tested setting, scored product, and broader work claim.

### [149] [Parallel Context Compaction for Long-Horizon LLM Agent Serving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23296)
*Musa Cim,Burak Topcu,Chita Das,Mahmut Taylan Kandemir*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出用于长程 LLM Agent 流程的并行上下文压缩方法，以替代传统顺序同步摘要，在相同压缩解码量下提升速度、吞吐，并增强摘要体量的可控性与可预测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长程 LLM Agent 会积累不断增长的对话历史，最终超出上下文窗口。现有基于 LLM 摘要的上下文压缩存在三类问题：摘要有损；同步阻塞调用会显著拖慢推理；操作者难以精细控制摘要长度，且不同运行中保留信息和输出 token 数波动大，导致知识保留不可预测。

Method: 作者提出 parallel compaction，将长上下文划分为多个块并行压缩，而非按顺序同步生成单一摘要。该方法允许针对不同块进行更细粒度的提示设计，并可通过块级控制实现更稳定的摘要体量。实验在 HotpotQA 多跳问答和 LoCoMo 长上下文对话基准上进行，覆盖 4 种 8B 到 120B 参数规模的模型骨干，包括 dense/MoE、reasoning/non-reasoning 模型。

Result: 在匹配压缩解码量的条件下，并行压缩相较顺序同步基线降低端到端墙钟时间，提高压缩吞吐量，同时提供更细粒度、更可预测的摘要体量控制。

Conclusion: 并行上下文压缩是长程 Agent 处理中更高效、可控且稳定的上下文管理方案，能够缓解传统 LLM 摘要压缩在延迟、体量控制和跨运行一致性方面的不足。

Abstract: Long-horizon LLM agents accumulate growing conversation histories that eventually exceed the model's context window. Context compaction via LLM-based summarization keeps the conversation bounded, but summarization is inherently lossy and the blocking call stalls agent inference for tens of seconds. Moreover, the operator has no fine-grained control over summary volume since prompt instructions are largely ignored, and as context grows, both the amount of output tokens the model produces and the information it retains fluctuate substantially from run to run, making the agent's retained knowledge unpredictable across runs. We introduce \textbf{parallel compaction} for long-horizon agentic flows and characterize it against the sequential synchronous baseline across four backbones spanning 8B to 120B parameters, mixing dense and MoE architectures with reasoning and non-reasoning models, on the HotpotQA multi-hop QA and LoCoMo long-context dialogue benchmarks. Parallel compaction gives the operator fine-grained, predictable control over summary volume and enables more targeted prompt engineering per block. At matched compaction decode volume, it reduces end-to-end wall time and improves compaction throughput over the sequential baseline.

### [150] [Ontological Knowledge Blocks: Executable Compliance and Profile-Based Validation for Trustworthy AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23297)
*Aasish Kumar Sharma,Julian M. Kunkel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 Ontological Knowledge Blocks（OKBs），将监管义务编译为可机器检查的约束，并在 AI 辅助 HPC 资源分配场景中验证其可行性与低延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 关键数字基础设施中的 AI 服务需要满足透明性、问责性、公平性和可追溯性等治理要求，但现有合规方式过度依赖文档、静态清单和人工审查，难以适配自动化 AI 系统的规模化验证需求。

Method: 作者形式化定义 OKB 为一个五元组，将规范性义务与 RDF/OWL 概念模式、可执行 SHACL 验证规则、显式证据需求以及 PROV-O 溯源链接绑定；并设计确定性监管编译器，将结构化中间表示（IR）记录转换为可组合知识库模块，支持基于治理 profile 的重配置。

Result: 在两个原型和 AI 辅助 HPC 资源分配场景中进行 24 次验证、覆盖四类治理 profile。结果显示验证具有 profile 敏感性，违规项呈严格加性累积，SHACL 验证延迟为 12.6–100.3 ms，profile 等价性测试确认 Combined 是最全面的 profile。

Conclusion: OKBs 为 AI 治理提供了一种可编程、可组合、可机器验证的合规基础设施，有望替代以文档为中心的人工审查模式，并支持服务代码不变情况下的治理策略重配置。

Abstract: AI-enabled services deployed in critical digital infrastructure are subject to governance obligations spanning transparency, accountability, fairness, and traceability. Compliance today remains documentation-centric: obligations are described in prose, audits rely on static checklists, and verification depends on manual review. Such approaches do not scale to automated AI systems. This paper introduces Ontological Knowledge Blocks (OKBs), a programmable governance infrastructure that compiles regulatory obligations into machine-checkable constraints over structured evidence graphs. We formalize an OKB as a 5-tuple that binds normative obligations to an RDF/OWL concept schema, executable SHACL validation rules, explicit evidence requirements, and PROV-O provenance links. A deterministic regulatory compiler translates structured Intermediate Representation (IR) records into composable KB modules, enabling profile-based governance reconfiguration without modifying service code. We implement two prototypes and evaluate them in an AI-assisted HPC resource allocation scenario across 24 validation runs and four governance profiles. Results demonstrate profile-sensitive validation, strictly additive violation accumulation, SHACL validation latency between 12.6 ms and 100.3 ms, and profile equivalence testing confirming Combined as the strictly most comprehensive profile. All artefacts are released as open source.

</details>


### [151] [DART: Semantic Recoverability for Structured Tool Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23311)
*Ke Yang,Panpan Li,Zonghan Wu,Kejin Xu,Huaxi Huang,Xiaoshui Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 DART，用于在结构化工具智能体中实现语义上安全的局部故障恢复，避免简单回滚破坏已提交的下游工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有运行时在失败恢复时面临安全但低效的全量重放与高效但可能语义不一致的局部检查点恢复之间的矛盾；尤其在下游消费者已基于上游输出采取行动的承诺敏感场景中，缺乏判断局部恢复是否仍然语义有效的标准。

Method: 作者形式化提出“语义可恢复性”概念，并设计模块化运行时 DART：定位失败实例，认证该实例的语义可恢复边界，将检查点与这些边界对齐，并在依赖约束和外部效果约束下选择可接受的恢复点；若不存在合法恢复点则阻止回滚。

Result: 在三个由 LLM 驱动的领域以及基于 LangGraph 的外部验证环境中，DART 在基线局部恢复失败的承诺敏感案例中均能正确恢复；五个领域的安全审计未发现被错误允许的不安全回滚。

Conclusion: 控制器层面的回滚合法性并不等同于语义有效性；要实现可靠的局部恢复，必须显式进行可接受性/语义可恢复性检查。

Abstract: When a structured tool agent fails mid-execution, the runtime faces a dilemma: replaying the entire task is safe but wasteful, while restoring from a local checkpoint is efficient but can leave committed downstream work tied to an upstream history that no longer exists. This tension is acute in commitment-sensitive settings, where rollback targets a single failed instance yet downstream consumers have already acted on its output. Existing recovery approaches provide mechanical rollback but no criterion for whether a local restore remains semantically valid after downstream commitment. We formalize this gap as semantic recoverability and address it in DART, a modular runtime that localizes the failed instance, certifies semantically recoverable boundaries of that instance, aligns checkpoints to those boundaries, and selects an admissible restore point that preserves committed downstream work under dependency and effect constraints-or blocks otherwise. Across three LLM-driven domains and external validation on a LangGraph-based substrate, DART correctly recovers all evaluated commitment-sensitive cases where baseline local recovery fails, and a five-domain safety audit finds no unsafe admitted rollbacks. These results show that controller legality does not imply semantic validity, and that sound local recovery requires an explicit admissibility check.

Abstract: Ventilator decision support requires sequential decisions that track evolving physiology and disease trajectories while respecting safety boundaries and clinician specific tuning styles. Rule based approaches rarely generalize personalization, and end to end reinforcement learning or single large language model systems remain difficult to control and audit. VDSS performs online preference adaptation with a contextual bandit, updating clinician specific preferences from the final accepted decision at each adjustment cycle and using them to guide subsequent recommendations. Structured rejection feedback triggers targeted replanning to reduce unproductive iterations and improve interaction stability. ### [153] [When Planning Fails Despite Correct Execution: On Epistemic Calibration for LLM-Based Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23414)
*Zehao Wang,Shilong Jin,Zhao Cao,Lanjun Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 EPC-AW，用于缓解基于 LLM 的多智能体系统在规划阶段因知识判断失准导致的计划可行性误判，并在实验中带来平均 9.75% 的系统成功率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统即使正确执行计划，也可能因智能体在规划时错误评估自身知识与信息充分性而失败。该问题不同于执行错误：它在规划阶段较为隐蔽，且会随新信息变化而动态演化，因此需要一种面向认知校准的规划机制。

Method: 作者提出 Epistemic Planning Calibration Agentic Workflow（EPC-AW）。该方法不直接验证计划可行性，而是考察计划在不同信息条件下是否仍获得支持；具体包括基于信息一致性的计划选择，以及一致性引导的认知状态精炼，用历史分歧信号指导后续规划校准。

Result: 实验表明，EPC-AW 将系统级任务成功率平均提升 9.75%。

Conclusion: EPC-AW 能有效缓解 LLM 多智能体规划中的认知失准问题，通过跨信息条件与跨智能体的一致性评估提升规划稳健性和系统成功率。

Abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems can fail even when planned actions are executed correctly because agents may misjudge their knowledge when evaluating plan feasibility, a phenomenon we term epistemic miscalibration in planning. Unlike execution errors, epistemic miscalibration is latent during planning, as generated plans can remain self-consistent and executable without observable errors; the miscalibration is also dynamic, as new information can alter feasibility assessments, potentially obscuring past miscalibration signals and causing them to recur over time. To address this, we propose the Epistemic Planning Calibration Agentic Workflow (EPC-AW), which assesses whether plans remain supported under varying information conditions rather than directly verifying feasibility. EPC-AW employs Information-consistency-based Plan Selection, selecting plans whose evaluations are stable across agents, together with Consistency-guided Epistemic State Refinement to adapt calibration over time by leveraging past discrepancies to guide future planning. Experiments show that EPC-AW improves system-level success by an average of 9.75%.

### [154] [EDGE-OPD: Internalizing Privileged Context with Evidence Guided On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23493)
*Aristotelis Lazaridis,Dylan Bates,Aman Sharma,Brian King,Vincent Lu,Jack FitzGerald*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文研究 On-Policy Self-Distillation 中特权上下文带来的副作用问题，提出 EDGE-OPD，通过引导式 rollout 与证据掩码，只在被特权信息支持的 token 位置更新学生模型，从而更可靠地迁移目标行为并减少能力退化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: OPSD 允许同一模型同时作为教师和学生，并在训练时向教师提供推理时不可见的特权上下文；但这些特权信息可能引起非目标行为变化，如推理方式、通用能力、回答长度、风格或局部 token 偏好变化，导致学生学习到副作用而非可迁移的目标行为。

Method: 作者提出 EviDence GuidEd On-Policy Distillation（EDGE-OPD）。其核心包括两点：一是使用 guided rollouts，在采样阶段将特权上下文诱导出的目标行为注入学生的 on-policy 数据；二是使用 evidence mask，仅在特权上下文能够支持所采样 token 的位置对学生进行更新，而不是对整个 rollout 的所有 token 更新。

Result: 实验表明，标准 OPSD 及其变体 RLSD（无论是否使用 verifier）在稀有 token/身份学习设置中都无法学会目标身份；加入 guided rollouts 后这些方法可以成功。掩码区域消融进一步显示，persona 信号主要集中在具有正证据支持的尾部区域。

Conclusion: EDGE-OPD 能更精确地将特权上下文中的目标行为迁移给学生模型，同时避免学生学习无关副作用，有助于提升知识迁移效率并保持通用能力。

Abstract: On-Policy Distillation (OPD) has gained wide attraction as an LLM post-training paradigm due to its effectiveness in improving capabilities without introducing model distribution drift, and consequently, regression in general tasks. On-Policy Self-Distillation (OPSD) is an efficient use-case of OPD, which is appealing as it requires only a single model as a student and teacher, and it also has the benefit of providing privileged context that is a absent at inference time (e.g. a persona, a private fact, or a worked solution) to the teacher during the training process. The challenge in this approach is that the privileged information can change model behavior more than intended: it can modify reasoning, degrade general capabilities, and affect performance indicators like response length, style, or local token preferences. Consequently, OPSD may train the student on side effects rather than a desired, transferable behavior. In this paper, we study this problem in a rare-token/identity setting and propose EviDence GuidEd On-Policy Distillation (EDGE-OPD), a modification of OPSD with two distinct characteristics: a) it uses guided rollouts to inject privileged-context behavior to the student at sampling time, so that the rare target behavior is actually present in the on-policy data, and b) it applies an evidence mask: the student is updated only at token positions where the privileged context supports the sampled token, rather than on every token in the rollout. We empirically show that OPSD (and its variant RLSD, with and without a verifier) completely fail to learn a target identity, while the integration of guided rollouts allows them to succeed. Additionally, mask-region ablations show that the persona signal is localized to the positive-evidence tail, allows us to draw valuable insights about efficient knowledge transfer and preservation of general purpose capabilities.

</details>

*Emma Legrand,Roger Kameugne,Pierre Schaus*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种将动态规划（DP）作为主搜索框架、约束规划（CP）作为传播子程序的混合方法，用于求解部分车间调度问题（PSSP）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上DP与CP通常分开使用；作者希望证明二者可以有效、优雅地结合，利用DP的搜索结构与CP的全局约束传播能力来处理复杂调度问题。

Method: 在已有PSSP纯DP方法基础上，将CP过滤算法嵌入DP搜索过程；支持anytime DP策略（如anytime column search），并利用CP建模灵活性处理任意优先约束图。此外，复用DP模型设计大邻域搜索（LNS），在重启间施加部分序调度以改进当前解。

Result: 该混合模型能够自然处理任意优先关系，并支持更灵活的搜索策略和LNS框架；但在该具体问题上性能尚不能与最先进的纯CP求解器竞争。

Abstract: Dynamic Programming (DP) and Constraint Programming (CP) are well-established paradigms for solving combinatorial optimization problems. Usually, these two approaches are used separately. This paper aims to show that the two can be combined effectively and elegantly, with DP serving as the primary search framework and CP used as a subroutine to leverage global constraint propagation. This paper presents such an approach for the Partial Shop Scheduling Problem (PSSP), for which a pure DP method has previously been proposed, and efficient CP filtering algorithms are available. The PSSP is a general scheduling problem where each job consists of a set of operations with arbitrary precedence constraints. The approach is flexible enough to accommodate anytime DP strategies, such as anytime column search, whereas the original DP algorithm operated in a strictly layer-wise manner. Moreover, the flexibility of the CP modeling makes it straightforward to incorporate arbitrary precedence constraints. As a result, the model naturally handles any precedence graph and even enables the design of a Large Neighborhood Search (LNS) scheme, in which the DP model is reused, and partial-order schedules are imposed across restarts to improve the incumbent solution. While not competitive with state-of-the-art pure CP solvers for this specific problem, our primary contribution is demonstrating the viability of this hybrid integration.

### [156] [Co-ReAct: Rubrics as Step-Level Collaborators for ReAct Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23590)
*Jiazheng Kang,Bowen Zhang,Zixin Song,Jiangwang Chen,Xiao Yang,Da Zhu,Guanjun Jiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 Co-ReAct：在 ReAct 智能体推理/检索的每一步注入由专门模型生成的细粒度 rubric，用作动作选择指导；该 rubric 生成器通过 GRPO 与基于专家共识排序的 list-wise Spearman 相关奖励训练，在多个深度研究与问答基准上优于 ReAct 和测试时计算基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 ReAct 式智能体在搜索密集、多步推理任务中主要依赖内部判断决定检索什么证据、下一步采取推理还是行动以及何时停止，容易产生浅层、重复或目标不明确的轨迹。已有 rubric 多用于训练奖励或事后评估，通常是报告级、粗粒度的，缺乏对推理过程每一步的直接指导。

Method: 作者提出 Co-ReAct，在每个决策步骤将 rubric 注入智能体上下文，指导下一步 Reason-or-Act 决策，明确证据搜寻、搜索、推理或自我评估的目标。为提升 rubric 质量，训练一个专用 rubric 生成器，并采用 GRPO；其目标不是二元或成对偏好，而是用 list-wise Spearman 秩相关奖励对齐多评审专家共识排序，鼓励生成具有区分性的 rubric。

Result: 在 DeepResearchBench 和 SQA-CS-V2 上，Co-ReAct 在基于 8B/14B 开源模型以及前沿闭源模型构建的搜索智能体中，均稳定优于 ReAct 和代表性测试时计算基线。训练好的 rubric 生成器还能作为即插即用模块，在不改变原有决策机制的情况下提升其他基线。

Conclusion: Co-ReAct 表明，将 rubric 从事后评价信号转化为推理时、步骤级的行动指导，可以显著改善搜索密集型多步推理智能体的轨迹质量与任务表现；基于专家排序训练的 rubric 生成器具有较好的泛化与模块化应用价值。

Abstract: ReAct-style agents for search-intensive, multi-step reasoning tasks rely largely on their own internal judgment to decide what evidence to seek, which reasoning or action step to take next, and when to stop, often producing shallow, redundant, or poorly targeted trajectories. Prior work has explored rubrics as external quality signals, but existing uses are mostly evaluative rather than action-guiding: rubrics typically serve as training-time rewards or post-hoc evaluators of completed outputs, and in deep-research settings they are often coarse-grained and report-level rather than step-level. We introduce Co-ReAct, a rubric-guided action-selection framework that uses rubrics as step-level guidance during inference. At each decision step, Co-ReAct injects a rubric into the agent's context to guide the next Reason-or-Act decision, specifying what the agent should target in evidence seeking, search, reasoning, or self-evaluation. To make this guidance reliable, we train a dedicated rubric generator with GRPO. Unlike prior pairwise or binary preference formulations, our objective optimizes a list-wise Spearman rank-correlation reward against multi-judge expert consensus rankings, encouraging rubrics that are discriminative rather than merely plausible. On DeepResearchBench and SQA-CS-V2, Co-ReAct consistently improves over ReAct and representative test-time compute baselines across search agents built on both 8B/14B open-source and frontier closed-source base models. The trained rubric generator can also serve as a drop-in component that improves these baselines without changing their underlying decision mechanisms. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/ZBWpro/Co-ReAct.

### [157] [One Policy, Infinite NPCs: Persona-Traceable Shared RL Policies for Scalable Game Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23652)
*Yoosung Hong*

Main category: cs.AI

Abstract: On a 300-persona life-simulation benchmark, pcsp achieves compositional zero-shot persona identification up to 17x above chance, Spearman rho approx 0.73 semantic-behavioral alignment, and 22x faster inference than an LLM-as-policy baseline. Life simulation games require hundreds to thousands of non-player characters (NPCs) that behave consistently with distinct personalities while remaining controllable through designer-authored natural language. Existing methods fail on constraints like persona consistency, controllability, or real-time inference. We introduce pcsp (Persona Conditioned Shared Policy), a single reinforcement learning policy conditioned on frozen LLM embeddings of free-form persona descriptions. pcsp combines once-per-NPC persona encoding, low-rank persona projection, neural persona conditioning, and a PPO + InfoNCE consistency + KL diversity training objective. Across three experimental settings, ablations show that the InfoNCE trajectory-consistency objective is load bearing: removing it collapses zero-shot persona identification to chance. External validation on Melting Pot 2.4.0 substrates confirms that our method produces persona-conditioned behavioral divergence in multi-agent strategic environments. We distinguish two senses of held-out evaluation: compositional zero-shot and vocabulary-expansion held-out. Finally, a UE5 deployment reproduces the in-engine persona-conditioning ablation at 64 agents with a low failure rate, showing that the sub-frame inference profile survives in a commercial game engine. These results prove that shared RL policies can support scalable, real-time, persona-conditioned NPC control.

### [158] [MemAudit: Post-hoc Auditing of Poisoned Agent Memory via Causal Attribution and Structural Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23723)
*Zhewen Tan,Yilun Yao,Huiyan Jin,Wenhan Yu,Guoan Wang,Mengyuan Fan,liang lu,Feng Liu,Xiangzheng Zhang,Duohe Ma,Tong Yang,Lin Sun*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 持久化记忆可提升 LLM Agent 的长期任务能力，但也带来安全风险：攻击者可通过普通交互向记忆库写入恶意记录，后续检索时影响模型推理与行动。现有防御多关注在线过滤或阻断，缺乏在有害行为发生后定位责任记忆的事后审计方法。

Method: MemAudit 结合两类信号：一是反事实记忆影响分数，用于衡量单条记忆对有害输出的因果贡献；二是记忆一致性图，用于在整体记忆库中发现结构异常记忆。论文在 MINJA 这种仅查询式记忆注入攻击下进行评估，该攻击通过正常交互生成并存储恶意记忆，而非直接篡改记忆库。

Result: 在问答和推理 Agent 场景中，MemAudit 在现实的事后审计设置下显著降低攻击成功率：QA 攻击成功率从 70% 降至 0%，RAP 攻击成功率从 83.3% 降至 0%。

Conclusion: MemAudit 表明，通过因果影响分析与结构一致性检测的结合，可以有效定位并清除导致有害行为的恶意记忆，为记忆增强型 LLM Agent 提供一种有效的事后安全审计机制。

Abstract: Large language model agents increasingly rely on persistent memory to store past interactions, retrieve relevant demonstrations, and improve long-horizon task execution. However, this memory mechanism also creates a practical security vulnerability: an adversarial user may inject malicious records into the agent's memory through ordinary interaction, and these records can later be retrieved to steer the agent's reasoning and actions. Existing defenses primarily focus on online intervention, such as prompt filtering or output blocking, but they do not address the post-hoc question of which stored memories are responsible after harmful behavior has already been observed. We propose \textbf{MemAudit}, a post-hoc causal memory auditing framework for memory-augmented LLM agents. The framework combines two complementary signals: (1) a counterfactual memory influence score that measures each memory's causal contribution to harmful outputs, and (2) a memory consistency graph that identifies structurally anomalous memories within the broader memory store. We evaluate MemAudit against MINJA, a query-only memory injection attack in which malicious records are generated and stored through normal agent interactions rather than direct memory-bank modification. Across both QA and reasoning-agent settings, MemAudit substantially reduces attack success rates under realistic post-hoc auditing scenarios. The results show that QA attack success is reduced from $70\%$ to $0\%$, while RAP attack success drops from $83.3\%$ to $0\%$.

</details>


### [159] [Agentic Proving for Program Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23772)
*Alessandro Sosso,Akhil Arora,Bas Spitters*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文评估 Claude Code 在 Lean 4 程序验证基准 CLEVER 上的智能体式证明能力，发现其在规格生成、实现验证和端到端生成验证流程中取得很高成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体系统已在形式化数学自动定理证明中表现突出，但其能力能否迁移到程序验证仍需系统评估；同时也需要检验现有程序验证基准是否仍具区分度。

Method: 作者将 Claude Code 置于智能体式证明框架中，在 Lean 4 的可验证代码生成基准 CLEVER 上评测多个阶段：生成规格、根据正确真值规格验证实现、以及端到端程序生成与验证；并结合 CLEVER 的同构评分和人工审查评估反馈质量与失败原因。

Result: Claude 为 98.8% 的问题生成了可认为有效的规格，其中 81.3% 被 CLEVER 的同构评分接受；在正确真值规格下对 87.5% 的问题完成实现认证；在前提自洽条目上端到端成功率达到 98.1%；其自我反馈经人工审查质量较高，并能发现失败原因和数据集残留缺陷。

Conclusion: 现代智能体证明器与现有程序验证基准难度之间出现不匹配，现有评测尤其是基于同构的规格评分存在局限；未来需要更严格、更抗数据缺陷的评测方法。整体上，紧密结合编译器反馈的智能体范式目前是基础程序验证中最有效的路径之一。

Abstract: Agentic systems have recently emerged as state-of-the-art approaches for automated theorem proving in formal mathematics. To assess how far these capabilities extend to program verification, we evaluate Claude Code in an agentic proving framework on CLEVER, a Lean 4 benchmark for verifiable code generation. Our results show that Claude generates arguably valid specifications for 98.8% of problems (with 81.3% also accepted by CLEVER's isomorphism-based scoring on the correct portion of the benchmark), certifies implementations against correct ground-truth specifications for 87.5% of problems, and reaches a 98.1% success rate on the end-to-end program generation and verification pipeline over entries with self-consistent premises. Across all stages, Claude further provides high-quality feedback on its own attempts (as confirmed under manual review), identifying underlying causes of failure and lingering bugs in the dataset. These findings highlight a growing mismatch between the difficulty of existing program verification benchmarks and the capabilities of modern agentic provers, and point to the need for more rigorous, bug-resilient evaluation methodologies, and in particular for alternatives to isomorphism-based scoring of generated specifications. More broadly, our results provide empirical evidence that tight compiler-in-the-loop agentic paradigms are currently the most effective approach for foundational program verification.

### [160] [Beyond Binary Edits Robust Multimodal Knowledge Editing with Adversarial Subspace Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23780)
*Haoyuan Wang,Xiaohao Liu,Jiajie Su,Jianmao Xiao,Chaochao Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出面向泛化性的鲁棒内在多模态知识编辑框架，通过语义等价知识单元、潜在空间对抗增强与低秩子空间约束，提升MLLM知识编辑在视觉与语言变体上的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有内在多模态知识编辑虽在可靠性与局部性方面表现较好，但对语义等价的图像或文本变体泛化不足，原因包括缺少显式语义监督、编辑范围僵硬，以及在高维多模态空间中过度锚定单一样本。

Method: 作者将鲁棒性形式化为由语义等价多模态输入组成的知识单元，并将泛化性定义为单元内预测一致性；提出LAR在联合潜在空间生成语义一致的对抗变体以暴露脆弱区域；提出RCSL在编辑层通过基于奇异值的目标约束对抗表征低秩对齐。

Result: 实验与分析表明，所提出的ASAM能够有效增强多模态知识编辑的泛化能力，同时面向鲁棒性目标改善对语义等价视觉和语言变化的预测一致性。

Conclusion: 该工作强调显式建模语义等价性与潜在空间鲁棒优化对于MLLM知识编辑泛化至关重要，ASAM为提升内在多模态知识编辑鲁棒性提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) need efficient mechanisms to update knowledge without degrading existing capabilities. While intrinsic multimodal knowledge editing achieves strong reliability and locality, it often exhibits limited generality, failing to propagate edits across semantically equivalent visual and linguistic variations. This issue arises from the lack of explicit semantic supervision, rigid editing scopes, and biased anchoring to individual samples in high-dimensional multimodal spaces. We address robust intrinsic multimodal knowledge editing by explicitly targeting generalization. We formalize robustness through knowledge units that group semantically equivalent multimodal inputs and define generality as consistent predictions within each unit. To expose fragile semantic regions, we introduce Latent Adversarial Robustification (LAR), which generates adversarial yet semantically coherent variants in the joint latent space. We further propose Rank-Constrained Subspace Learning (RCSL), enforcing low-rank alignment of adversarial representations at the edit layer via a singular value-based objective. Extensive analysis demonstrates the effectiveness of ASAM empirically.

### [161] [SPACENUM: Revisiting Spatial Numerical Understanding in VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23898)
*Jianshu Zhang,Yijiang Li,Huifeixin Chen,Haoran Lu,Letian Xue,Bingyang Wang,Han Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 SpaceNum 框架，用 Num2Space 与 Space2Num 双向任务评估 VLM 在动态探索与静态布局中的空间数值 grounding 能力，发现现有模型普遍接近随机、依赖浅层线索，微调可带来部分改善。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM 越来越多用于具身环境，需要输出动作幅度、空间坐标等数值；但这些数值是否真正建立在空间感知与空间表征之上尚不清楚，因此需要系统评估其空间数值理解能力。

Method: 作者提出统一评测框架 SpaceNum，覆盖两类互补场景：动态空间探索中的数值转移，以及静态空间推理中的布局数值。构造 Num2Space 与 Space2Num 两个双向任务，测试模型在视觉空间结构与语言数值表示之间的映射能力，并结合错误分析、推理轨迹分析和受控干预研究模型行为。

Result: 实验显示，在动态转移和静态布局任务中，当前 VLM 大多无法将数值与空间含义可靠绑定，表现常接近随机猜测；模型倾向依赖浅层空间线索，难以形成稳定的坐标感知表征，也难以从视觉观察中抽象结构化空间布局。显式推理仅带来有限收益，而微调能部分提升空间数值理解，并迁移到外部空间推理基准。

Conclusion: 现有 VLM 的数值输出并不充分 grounded 于空间感知，尤其在坐标、距离、动作幅度等具身相关数值任务中存在明显短板。SpaceNum 揭示了空间数值理解评估的重要性，并表明需要更强的坐标表征、结构化空间抽象和针对性训练来提升 VLM 的具身空间能力。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) are increasingly deployed in embodied environments, where they need produce numerical outputs such as action magnitudes and spatial coordinates. Although these numbers appear meaningful, it remains unclear whether these numerical outputs are genuinely grounded in spatial perception. Therefore, in this work, we revisit spatial numerical understanding through SpaceNum, a unified framework that captures two complementary settings: numbers as dynamic transitions during spatial exploration, and numbers as static layouts in spatial reasoning. We formulate two bidirectional tasks, Num2Space and Space2Num, to evaluate how well VLMs map between vision-side spatial structure and language-side numerical representations. We systematically study whether current VLMs truly understand numerical values in spatial settings. Across dynamic transitions and static layouts, we find that models largely fail to ground numbers in spatial meaning and often perform close to random guess. Through error analysis, reasoning trace analysis, and controlled interventions, we show that current VLMs rely heavily on shallow spatial cues, struggle to build stable coordinate-aware representations, and fail to abstract structured spatial layouts from visual observations. We further show that explicit reasoning provides only marginal gains, while tuning can partially improve spatial numerical understanding and transfer to external spatial reasoning benchmarks.
